Added checks for `soft_time_limit` and `time_limit`:
- In `celery/app/task.py`, added a check to ensure `soft_time_limit` does not exceed `time_limit`.
- In `t/integration/tasks.py`, added a wrapper function `soft_time_limit_must_exceed_time_limit` to handle `soft_time_limit` and `time_limit` settings.
- In `t/integration/test_tasks.py`, added tests to verify the new logic.

These changes are necessary to prevent errors related to incorrect task time limit configurations.

Fixes #9125
